  function get_mapped_ad_unit_value(ad_unit_name, map, ssp) {
    participants1[ssp]=&quot;0&quot;;
	if (map[ad_unit_name]) {
		var savemap = map[ad_unit_name];
		if (savemap[&quot;728x90&quot;] || savemap[&quot;640x480&quot;] || savemap [&quot;160x600&quot;] || savemap[&quot;300x250&quot;]){
		   placement = savemap[dfp_width.toString()+&quot;x&quot;+dfp_height.toString()];
		} else {
		   placement = map[ad_unit_name];
		}
	} else if (map.default) {
		var savemap = map.default;
		if (savemap[&quot;728x90&quot;] || savemap[&quot;640x480&quot;] || savemap [&quot;160x600&quot;] || savemap[&quot;300x250&quot;]) {
			placement = savemap[dfp_width.toString()+&quot;x&quot;+dfp_height.toString()];
		} else {
		placement =  savemap;
		}
	} else {
		console.log(&quot;No mapping entries exist for map!!&quot;);
		placement = &quot;&quot;;
	}
	return placement;
  }

function custom_price_bucket(bidResponse){var cpm=bidResponse.cpm;if(cpm&lt;4.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*50)/50).toFixed(2)}else if(cpm&lt;8.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*20)/20).toFixed(2)}else if(cpm&lt;20.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*10)/10).toFixed(2)}else if(cpm&lt;69.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*1)/1).toFixed(2)}else{return &quot;70.00&quot;}}

function buildparticipants(){
	var order1 = [&quot;appnexus&quot;,&quot;rubicon&quot;,&quot;pubmatic&quot;,&quot;criteo&quot;,&quot;indexExchange&quot;];
	var parts = &quot;&quot;;
	var ssp;
	for (var i in order1){
		ssp = order1[i];
		if(ssp in participants1){
			parts = parts + participants1[ssp];
		}
	}
	return parts;
}

  pbjs.bidderSettings = {

&lt;script&gt; 

      &lt;!-- GPT CONFIG --&gt;
      var gptadslots = [];
      var googletag = googletag || {};
      googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
      googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
      });

      pbjs.que.push(function() {
        pbjs.addAdUnits(adUnits);
        pbjs.requestBids({
		  bidsBackHandler: sendAdserverRequest
		});
	  })

      function sendAdserverRequest() {
        if (pbjs.adserverRequestSent) return;
        pbjs.adserverRequestSent = true;
        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
          pbjs.que.push(function() {
			if (output_flag==1){
				console.log(dfp_ad_unit+': '+'setting dfp key-values')
			}
            pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
			participants = buildparticipants();
			if (output_flag=1){
			console.log('END:'+dfp_ad_unit+': '+&quot;hb_bid_status is &quot;+bid_status+&quot;. final hb_participants is &quot;+participants+&quot;. dealflag is &quot;+dealflag);
			}
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_bid_status&quot;,bid_status);
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_participants&quot;,participants);
            try{
            	googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_test&quot;,testnum1.toString());
        	}
        	catch(err){
            }
            try{
            	googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_test2&quot;,testnum2.toString());
        	}
        	catch(err){
            }

randomAdGroup = function() {
var rand = Math.random();
	switch (false) {
		case !(rand &lt; 0.09): return &quot;ad_ex&quot; + (Math.floor(100 * rand));
		case !(rand &lt; 0.10): return &quot;ad_bc&quot;;
		default: return &quot;ad_opt&quot;;
	}
};

	usd_to_aud_fx = storagetest;
	console.log('using stored fx... '+storagetest);
} else {
	var request_url=&quot;https://query.yahooapis.com/v1/public/yql?q=select%20*%20from%20yahoo.finance.xchange%20where%20pair%20in%20(%22USDAUD%22)&amp;format=json&amp;diagnostics=false&amp;env=store%3A%2F%2Fdatatables.org%2Falltableswithkeys&amp;callback=&quot;;
	var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
	var t2 = performance.now();
	xhr.open('GET', request_url,true);
	xhr.send();
	xhr.addEventListener(&quot;readystatechange&quot;,processRequest,false);
	console.log('get new fx...');
	function processRequest(e){
		if (xhr.readyState==4 &amp;&amp; xhr.status==200){
			var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
			if (output_flag==1){
				var t3 = performance.now();
				console.log(dfp_ad_unit+': '+'usd to aud response is '+ response.query.results.rate.Bid+'. Response took '+(t3-t2)+' milliseconds.');
			}
			usd_to_aud_fx=response.query.results.rate.Bid;
			sessionStorage.setItem('fxrate',usd_to_aud_fx);
			sessionStorage.setItem('fxdate',todaydate);
		}else if(xhr.status==400){
			console.log(dfp_ad_unit+': '+'yahoo finance error code: 400');
		}
	}
}

            node.parentNode.appendChild(dpf);
    }

  function get_mapped_ad_unit_value(ad_unit_name, map, ssp) {
    participants1[ssp]=&quot;0&quot;;
	if (map[ad_unit_name]) {
		var savemap = map[ad_unit_name];
		if (savemap[&quot;728x90&quot;] || savemap[&quot;640x480&quot;] || savemap [&quot;160x600&quot;] || savemap[&quot;300x250&quot;]){
		   placement = savemap[dfp_width.toString()+&quot;x&quot;+dfp_height.toString()];
		} else {
		   placement = map[ad_unit_name];
		}
	} else if (map.default) {
		var savemap = map.default;
		if (savemap[&quot;728x90&quot;] || savemap[&quot;640x480&quot;] || savemap [&quot;160x600&quot;] || savemap[&quot;300x250&quot;]) {
			placement = savemap[dfp_width.toString()+&quot;x&quot;+dfp_height.toString()];
		} else {
		placement =  savemap;
		}
	} else {
		console.log(&quot;No mapping entries exist for map!!&quot;);
		placement = &quot;&quot;;
	}
	return placement;
  }

function custom_price_bucket(bidResponse){var cpm=bidResponse.cpm;if(cpm&lt;4.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*50)/50).toFixed(2)}else if(cpm&lt;8.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*20)/20).toFixed(2)}else if(cpm&lt;20.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*10)/10).toFixed(2)}else if(cpm&lt;69.00){return(Math.floor(cpm*1)/1).toFixed(2)}else{return &quot;70.00&quot;}}

function buildparticipants(){
	var order1 = [&quot;appnexus&quot;,&quot;rubicon&quot;,&quot;pubmatic&quot;,&quot;criteo&quot;,&quot;indexExchange&quot;];
	var parts = &quot;&quot;;
	var ssp;
	for (var i in order1){
		ssp = order1[i];
		if(ssp in participants1){
			parts = parts + participants1[ssp];
		}
	}
	return parts;
}

      function sendAdserverRequest() {
        if (pbjs.adserverRequestSent) return;
        pbjs.adserverRequestSent = true;
        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
          pbjs.que.push(function() {
			if (output_flag==1){
				console.log(dfp_ad_unit+': '+'setting dfp key-values')
			}
            pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
			participants = buildparticipants();
			if (output_flag=1){
			console.log('END:'+dfp_ad_unit+': '+&quot;hb_bid_status is &quot;+bid_status+&quot;. final hb_participants is &quot;+participants+&quot;. dealflag is &quot;+dealflag);
			}
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_bid_status&quot;,bid_status);
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_participants&quot;,participants);
            try{
            	googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_test&quot;,testnum1.toString());
        	}
        	catch(err){
            }
            try{
            	googletag.pubads().setTargeting(&quot;hb_test2&quot;,testnum2.toString());
        	}
        	catch(err){
            }
            googletag.pubads().refresh();
          });
        });
      }

        sendAdserverRequest();
